	[user_user] [nvarchar](8) NULL,

	[kann_bis] [datetime] NULL,
	[mail] [bit] NULL,

	[acd_passwort] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[frmd_id] [int] NULL,
	[provision] [float] NULL,
	[freistellung] [bit] NULL,
	[adr_id] [int] NULL,

	[last_name_ru] [nvarchar](80) NULL,

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[abos](
	[id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[adr_id] [int] NULL,
	[bst_id] [int] NOT NULL,
	[bks_id] [int] NOT NULL,
	[object_id] [int] NULL,
	[bezeichnung] [nvarchar](120) NULL,
	[ausgaben] [int] NOT NULL,
	[erstellt_am] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	[beginnt_am] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	[geändert_am] [datetime] NULL,
	[status_id] [int] NOT NULL,
	[flag] [bit] NULL,
	[SSMA_TimeStamp] [timestamp] NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [abos$PrimaryKey] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[id] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
